# Debt Protocol · Chapter 12 · Chain of Noise

**File:** `media/novel/ch12-pNN.png` (match `NN` to panel id, e.g. `novel-p12` → `ch12-p12.png`).

## How to use these prompts
1. Copy the **Full prompt** for one panel into your image model as the **scene + art direction** positive (action, environment, lighting intent, readability, and framing).
2. Add **rendering medium and look** yourself—brush style, film grain, painterly vs clean line, palette, and any extra “no text” reinforcement—in a preset or a second positive block.
3. Match aspect ratio to **Layout** (wide splash vs tall tier).
4. Keep speech balloons off the render if you composite them in post; the site supplies balloon text separately.

---

## novel-p1 · page 1 · span-12

**Layout:** wide splash (~2:1 landscape). One strong establishing image; leave lower third relatively open for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
The legal drone didn’t wait for the crowd to finish being alive.
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel: The legal drone didn’t wait for the crowd to finish being alive. Art direction: grounded near-future sci-fi production design; clear focal hierarchy and readable silhouettes; directional practical light with motivated shadows; believable wear on materials; leave calm negative space where dialogue balloons composite in post; do not letter speech or captions inside the frame. Wide cinematic composition, landscape, strong environment read.

**Tracking (for filenames / sheets, not part of the image prompt):**

Chapter 12, Chain of Noise, panel 1, comic page 1

**Layout:** vertical tier panel (~4:5 portrait). Tight readable focal; leave margin for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
[INTEGRITY AUDIT  /  LIVE]

Participant may rebut with verified exhibits
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel: [INTEGRITY AUDIT / LIVE] Scope: checksum chain + injection event Burden: station must demonstrate chain integrity Participant may rebut with verified exhibits Holographic HUD overlay: simple lines and symbols, abstract data shapes, not a wall of tiny readable text. Art direction: grounded near-future sci-fi production design; clear focal hierarchy and readable silhouettes; directional practical light with motivated shadows; believable wear on materials; leave calm negative space where dialogue balloons composite in post; do not letter speech or captions inside the frame. Screen glow and HUD readouts stay abstract—no micro-legible text blocks. Vertical comic panel, portrait emphasis, figure and set readable at a glance.

## novel-p34 · page 16 · span-4

**Layout:** vertical tier panel (~4:5 portrait). Tight readable focal; leave margin for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

